**哺乳动物分类表**是根据[动物分类学的方法列出的各种](../Page/动物分类学.md "wikilink")[哺乳动物的分类](../Page/哺乳动物.md "wikilink")。在[属下每个物种举一个例子来说明](../Page/属.md "wikilink")。

哺乳动物在分类学上称为[哺乳纲](../Page/哺乳纲.md "wikilink")。以下就是这一[纲的分类列表](../Page/纲.md "wikilink")。

*注：†表示已絕種*

## [原獸亞綱](../Page/原獸亞綱.md "wikilink")(Prototheria)

### [单孔目](../Page/单孔目.md "wikilink") Monotremata

  - [寒地掘地兽属](../Page/寒地掘地兽属.md "wikilink") †*Kryoryctes* Pridmore, Rich,
    Vickers-Rich & Gambaryan, 2005
      - †*Kryoryctes cadburyi* Pridmore, Rich, Vickers-Rich & Gambaryan,
        2005
  - [扁足亚目](../Page/扁足亚目.md "wikilink") Platypoda Gill, 1872
      - [十字齿兽科](../Page/十字齿兽科.md "wikilink") †Kollikodontidae\[nota 3\]
        Flannery, Archer, Rich & Jones, 1995
          - [十字齿兽屬](../Page/十字齿兽屬.md "wikilink") †*Kollikodon* Flannery,
            Archer, Rich & Jones, 1995
              - †*Kollikodon ritchiei* Flannery, Archer, Rich & Jones,
                1995
      - [硬齒鴨嘴獸科](../Page/硬齒鴨嘴獸科.md "wikilink") †Steropodontidae Archer,
        Flannery, Ritchie & Molnar, 1985
          - [硬齒鴨嘴獸屬](../Page/硬齒鴨嘴獸屬.md "wikilink") †*Steropodon* Archer,
            Flannery, Ritchie & Molnar, 1985
              - †*Steropodon galmani* Archer, Flannery, Ritchie &
                Molnar, 1985
          - [泰诺脊齿兽屬](../Page/泰诺脊齿兽屬.md "wikilink") †*Teinolophos* Rich,
            Vickers-Rich, Constantine, Flannery, Kool & van Klaveren,
            1999
              - †*Teinolophos trusleri* Rich, Vickers-Rich, Constantine,
                Flannery, Kool & van Klaveren, 1999
      - [鸭嘴兽科](../Page/鸭嘴兽科.md "wikilink") Ornithorhynchidae Gray, 1825
          - [鸭嘴兽屬](../Page/鸭嘴兽屬.md "wikilink") *Ornithorhynchus*
            Blumenbach, 1800
              - [鸭嘴兽](../Page/鸭嘴兽.md "wikilink") *Ornithorhynchus
                anatinus* (Shaw, 1799)
          - [顽齿鸭嘴兽屬](../Page/顽齿鸭嘴兽屬.md "wikilink") †*Obdurodon*
            Woodburne & Tedford, 1975
              - †*Obdurodon dicksoni* Archer, Jenkins, Hand, Murray &
                Godthelp, 1992
              - †*Obdurodon insignis* Woodburne & Tedford, 1975
          - [單孔屬](../Page/單孔屬.md "wikilink") †*Monotrematum* Pascual,
            Archer, Ortiz, Jaureguizar, Prado, Godthelp & Hand, 1992（=
            Obdurodon）
              - †*Monotrematum sudamericanum* Pascual, Archer, Ortiz,
                Jaureguizar, Prado, Godthelp & Hand, 1992
  - [速舌亚目](../Page/速舌亚目.md "wikilink") Tachyglossa Gill, 1872
      - [针鼹科](../Page/针鼹科.md "wikilink") Tachyglossidae Gill, 1872
          - [针鼹屬](../Page/针鼹屬.md "wikilink") *Tachyglossus* Illiger,
            1811
              - [澳洲针鼹](../Page/澳洲针鼹.md "wikilink") ''Tachyglossus
                aculeatus (Shaw, 1792)
          - [原針鼹屬](../Page/原針鼹屬.md "wikilink") *Zaglossus* Gill, 1872
              - [阿滕伯勒長喙針鼴鼠](../Page/阿滕伯勒長喙針鼴鼠.md "wikilink") *Zaglossus
                attenboroughi* Flannery & Groves, 1998
              - [長吻针鼹](../Page/長吻针鼹.md "wikilink") *Zaglossus brujini*
                (Peters & Doria, 1876)
              - [大長吻針鼴](../Page/大長吻針鼴.md "wikilink") *Zaglossus bartoni*
                Thomas, 1907
              - †*Zaglossus hacketti* (Glauert, 1914)
              - †*Zaglossus robustus* (Dun, 1895)
          - [巨针鼹屬](../Page/巨针鼹屬.md "wikilink") †*Megalibgwilia*
            Griffiths, Wells & Barrie, 1991
              - †*Megalibgwilia robusta* (Dun, 1986)
              - †*Megalibgwilia ramsayi* (Owen, 1884)

  - [鼠狐猴科](../Page/鼠狐猴科.md "wikilink")（Cheirogaleidae）

            *）：[中棘鼠](../Page/中棘鼠.md "wikilink")（*Mesomys
            didelphoides ''）
          - [地棘鼠屬](../Page/地棘鼠屬.md "wikilink")（''Proechimys

            albispinus ''）
          - [隱棘鼠屬](../Page/隱棘鼠屬.md "wikilink")（''Thrichomys
            *）：[隱棘鼠](../Page/隱棘鼠.md "wikilink")（*Thrichomys
            apereoides ''）
      - [穴鼠亞科](../Page/穴鼠亞科.md "wikilink")（Heteropsomyinae）
